$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / For Loops Counting1

::For Loops Level 1 #000::
How many times does the '*' print?
<pre>for (int j = 12; j <= 34; j = j + 5)
\{
	cout << '*' << " ";
\}</pre>	{
	=5
	~4
	~6
	~1
	~7
	}

	=4
	~3
	~5
	~-2
	~0
	}
